--
-- Table structure for table `rooms`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `rooms`;
CREATE TABLE `rooms` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `sfsroomid` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `roomPWD` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `creator` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `creatorName` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `startat` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `players` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `gamestarted` bit(1) NOT NULL,
  `roundnum` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `createDate` datetime default NULL,
  `exhaustedDate` datetime default NULL,
  `exhausted` bit(1) NOT NULL,
  `game_id` bigint(20) default NULL,
  `hidden` tinyint(1) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FK67A9AF820898D49` (`game_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=433 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

--
-- Table structure for table `sessions`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `sessions`;
CREATE TABLE `sessions` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `sessionid` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `username` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `authticket` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `startTime` datetime default NULL,
  `lastRequestTime` datetime default NULL,
  `gamename` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `vkontakteid` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `vkontaktefrnds` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `locationid` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `roomcreator` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `lifetime` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `exhausted` bit(1) NOT NULL,
  `profile_id` bigint(20) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  KEY `FK53BFD09DE54EC5EB` (`profile_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=772 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
